       trulia.ready(function () {

  $('.toggleModalRightColumn').on('click', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();

    $('.toggleModalRightColumn').show();
    $(this).hide();

    if ($('.rightPanel').is(':hidden'))
    {
      $('.rightPanel').show();
      $('.modalActions').css('width', '300px');
      $('.visibilityCol').removeClass('cols17').addClass('cols19');
      o_track_ql_click('PhotoPlayerModal|ShowPanel');
    }
    else
    {
      $('.modalActions').css('width', '200px');
      $('.visibilityCol').removeClass('cols19').addClass('cols17');
      $('.rightPanel').hide();
      o_track_ql_click('PhotoPlayerModal|HidePanel');
    }

    $(window).trigger('resize'); 
  });

  $('.closePhotoModal').on('click', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();

    o_track_ql_click('PhotoPlayerModal|CloseModalButton');
    $('#photoPlayerModal').modal('close');
  });

});
      </script>

       <div class="aside asideFloater mln">
        <div id="ssa_container">
         <div class="ad300x250flex" id="trulia_ssa" style="position:relative; top: 12px">
         </div>
         <div class="clearfix" id="trulia_ssa">
          <script type="text/javascript">
           trulia.ready(function()
  {
    var original_key = 'trulia_ssa'
      , fallback_key = 'trulia_ssa_backfill'
      ;

    /* adds targeting to the ad url */
    function addTargeting(url)
    {
      try
      {
        if (!_AD_TARGETING || typeof(_AD_TARGETING) == 'undefined')
        {
          return url;
        }
        /* Don't overwrite existing query keys */
        var set_keys = {};
        var split_url = url.split('?');
        if (split_url.length == 2)
        {
          var query_params = split_url[1].split('&amp;');
          for (var i = 0; i &lt; query_params.length; i++)
          {
            set_keys[query_params[i].split('=')[0]] = true;
          }
        }
        /**/
        var ad_targeting = _AD_TARGETING;
        var ad_targeting_string = '';
        for(var name in ad_targeting)
        {
          if (ad_targeting.hasOwnProperty(name) &amp;&amp; ad_targeting[name] != null &amp;&amp; !set_keys[name])
          {
            ad_targeting_string += name + '=' + encodeURIComponent(ad_targeting[name]) + '&amp;';
          }
        }
        ad_targeting_string = ad_targeting_string.substr(0, ad_targeting_string.length - 1);
        return url + '&amp;' + ad_targeting_string;
      }
      catch (e) /*malformed url, fail gracefully */
      {
        return url;
      }
    }

    function fetchAd(url)
    {
      /* request ad, jsonp way */
      $.getJSON(addTargeting(url)+'&amp;callback=?', function(result)
      {
        /* check for ad results */
        if (!result || result.status != 'ok')
        {
          /* trigger event with div's id */
          $('#'+original_key)
            .html('')
            .attr('id', fallback_key)
            ;
          /* notify parties, tell we should fallback */
          $(document).trigger('ads:'+fallback_key, {fallback: true});
          return;
        }

        /* check for SSA placeholder */
        if (!$('#'+original_key).length &amp;&amp; $('#'+fallback_key).length)
        {
          /* rename it and clean up */
          $('#'+fallback_key).attr('id', original_key);
        }

        /* add iframe to the div */
        $('#'+original_key).html(unescape(result.data.container));
        /* set ad url */
        $('#'+original_key+' iframe').attr('src', unescape(result.data.url));

        /* notify parties, tell we should NOT fallback */
        $(document).trigger('ads:'+fallback_key, {fallback: false});
      });
    }

    /* trigger ad */
    fetchAd('http://spotlight.trulia.com/self_service.js?truliaads=1&amp;city=Copley&amp;state=OH&amp;zip=44321&amp;channel=trulia&amp;context=pdp%2Cfor+sale&amp;site_id=120056&amp;feed_id=3037&amp;is_foreclosure=0&amp;acting_uid=&amp;r=490918064&amp;co=n&amp;_k=1943cd0a4f950c7bd8bab14bcdcc2da4');

    /* add listener if ad should be refreshed */
    $(document).on('ads:'+original_key, function(e, url)
    {
      if (!url) return;

      fetchAd(url);
    });

  });
          </script>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </aside>

       Minor Rd
      </a>
